<user_name>The Rez Show</user_name>< review>
Graduated student from Milan. This school was amazing. The instructors are very helpful, the curriculum was on point. Almost everyone who graduates from here has passed their state board. I would say 80-90% of graduating students. This school also pays for your state board kit, which is not included at other schools.
As for the salon floor. There is very limited teaching staff. 3 teachers to 100 students. They do what they can. The wait and work is a little longer, but hey they are students. All of my clients had loved their experience and have returned my whole time while on the salon floor.  Please people. Let the students do their work. I have nothing bad to say about this school. I have spent 10 hrs a day here for 13 months and have enjoyed my entire experience. I would recommend this school to anyone. And as for the salon i would say, just be patient with the students.< /review>

We searched the web and found Menifee Collision center and gave them a call. < Review>
Xyclo began serving banh mi during the pandemic and they are *excellent*. The best vegetarian banh mi I've had in the Bay Area. The addition of mushroom and sweet potato add a nice complexity to the fried tofu. They're not particularly cheap at $7.95, but they are tastier and more substantial than most. Unless you're really hungry, you can stretch one into two meals. You can also add a Thai tea or Vietnamese coffee for $2, which helps offset the sandwich price. Both are really good.< /Review>

I don't normally leave reviews, but I feel it is important to share how great BioSport is. Other reviews are true when they say the staff became their friends instead of just their therapists. I honestly look forward to my sessions, and I always know I'm going to have a good laugh while I'm there. I am very active in my healing process, and everyone, especially Alex and Leo, are very helpful in teaching me how to maintain my progress. See, I was born with weak ankles, that coupled with poor shoes, have led to falling arches and tendon dysfunction. This in return causes pain when I run or exercise. This pain hinders my career goals. However, thanks to the knowledge, patience, kindness, and friendship of the entire BioSport team, I have a FAR better understanding of my situation and how I can work to counteract the damage done in my foot and ankle. I've been working with the BioSport team for over six weeks now, and I still have another six to go. Within my first six weeks, BioSport got my ankles to normal strength! My calves and ankles have never felt so strong. There is still more progress to be done, but I trust that the BioSport team will have no problem getting me to where I need to be. They're innovative, knowledgeable, and they really do apply the "one on one approach."

If you are looking for a place that will make you comfortable and provide great treatment, then BioSport is the place for you!

<Review>Man. It's a small Churches Chicken. I was kinda stunned at first compared to what I'm used to. There isn't a drive thru, wait near the door if you wanna stay cool (it's very hot in there), and they have coupons online y'all that are better than their in store deals.
